***дарить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дарить.html>дари́ть</a> (5685)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дар.html>дар</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dar</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дарить.html>дари́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">darítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подарить.html>подари́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to give, to make a present, to present, to donate</li>
<li>to favour, to bestow, to award</li></ol>

***дармовой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дармовой.html>дармово́й</a> (20484)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дармовой.html>дармово́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">darmovój</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>free (of charge), gratuitous</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дармовой.html>дармово́й</a></b>

***даровать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:даровать.html>дарова́ть</a> (13108)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дар.html>дар</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dar</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:даровать.html>дарова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">darovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">lofty</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to grant
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:даровать.html>дарова́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:прощение.html>проще́ние</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>darovátʹ</b> proščénije komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">grant somone one's pardon</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:даровать.html>дарова́ть</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:свобода.html>свобо́ду</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жизнь</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>darovátʹ</b> komú-libo svobódu (žiznʹ)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">grant someone his liberty (life)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, двувидовой (<a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:образовывать.html>образо́вывать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рмы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a>), <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:датчанин.html>датча́нин</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">datčánin</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:датчанин.html>датча́нина</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:датчанин.html>датча́не</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:датчанин.html>датча́н</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">датча́нка</b>)

***дать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a> (179)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dati</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*dṓˀtei</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dédeh₃ti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to give</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">donate</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">date</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">data</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">datʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to give
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>Да́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:холодильник.html>холоди́льник</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Daj</b> mne xolodílʹnik!</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>give</b> me a refrigerator!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to let, to allow
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>Да́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> порули́ть!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Daj</b> mne porulítʹ!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Please <b>allow</b> me to drive!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to organize, to create
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>Как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:странный.html>стра́нно</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дади́м</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:настоящий.html>настоя́щий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:восток.html>восто́к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:искусство.html>иску́сстве</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kak éto ni stránno, a my <b>dadím</b> nastojáščij Vostók v iskússtve.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">As strange as it seems, <b>we'll conjure</b> the true Orient in art. -Scriabin</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to hit, to strike, to clip, to give it to someone
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> б <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja b jemú tak <b>dál</b> za éto!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I'd have <b>given it</b> to him for that!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">idiomatic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to estimate someone's age from their appearance
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:можно.html>мо́жно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> бо́льше <a href = vnd.unilang:сорок.html>сорока́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Na vid jemú móžno býlo <b>datʹ</b> ne bólʹše soroká.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">From his appearance it was impossible to <b>suppose</b> that he was over forty.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дади́те</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Skólʹko vy mne <b>dadíte</b> let?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">How old do you <b>think</b> I am?</span></div></dd></dl>

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>вот</a> нафига́ <a href = vnd.unilang:вчера.html>вчера́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дала́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:первый.html>пе́рвое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свидание.html>свида́ние</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">A vot nafigá včerá <b>dalá</b> v pérvoje že svidánije?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">And why <b>did</b> you <b>have sex</b> yesterday on the first date?</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Negative forms with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> feature alternative stress on the particle in standard Russian for masculine, neuter and plural forms past tense and past passive short participles: "<a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́л</a>" and "<a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́л</a>", "<a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дало</a>" and "<a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дало́</a>", "<a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дали</a>" and "<a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́ли</a>"; "<a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:данный.html>дан</a>" and "<a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:данный.html>да́н</a>", "<a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:данный.html>дано́</a>" and "<a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:данный.html>дано́</a>", "<a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:данный.html>даны́</a>" and "<a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:данный.html>даны́</a>".</li></ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">datʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:даться.html>да́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:даваться.html>дава́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to let oneself, to allow oneself (to be caught, to be cheated, etc.)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:даваться.html>дава́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обида.html>оби́ду</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>davátʹsja</b> v obídu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">not to allow oneself to be pushed around/over</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to come easily
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:даваться.html>даю́тся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:иностранный.html>иностра́нные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>языки́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jemú ne <b>dajútsja</b> inostránnyje jazykí.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Foreign languages don't come easily to him.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">datʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́ть</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — ^b/c".     <a href = vnd.unilang:ударение.html>Ударе́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рмы</a> прош. вр. м. р. ед. ч. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:даться.html>дался́</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:являться.html>явля́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:устаревший.html>устаре́вшим</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:даваться.html>дава́ться</a>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дача.html>да́ча</a> (1514)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*daťa</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dati</i> (whence <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">datʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дача.html>да́ча</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dáča</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дача.html>да́чи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дача.html>да́чи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дача.html>да́ч</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dacha, villa, country house</li>
<li>a (small) plot of land in the outskirts of Russian cities usually used by city dwellers for growing fruit and vegetables</li>
<li>giving
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дача.html>да́ча</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:показание.html>показа́ний</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dáča pokazánij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">giving evidence, testifying, deposition, statement</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выдача.html>вы́дача</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">výdača</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дачник.html>да́чник</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dáčnik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дачный.html>да́чный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dáčnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***дачка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дачка.html>да́чка</a> (22087)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Diminutive of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dъ̏ťi</i> (cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk"><a href = vnd.unilang:дочка.html>дочка́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dočká</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дочка.html>до́чка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dóčka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*duktē</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰugh₂tḗr</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="be"><a href = vnd.unilang:дачка.html>дачка́</a></strong> • (<span lang="be-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dačká</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="be">дачкі́</b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="be">до́чкі</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>daughter</li></ol>

***два.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a> (75)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dъva</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dwóh₁</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral_4">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dva</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>две</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>two (2)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a></b></i> and <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>две</a></b></i>, when in the nominative case or accusative case, even in compounds (22, 32, 42, 102, etc.), govern the genitive of the noun.<i></i>
</p>
<dl><dd><ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчика</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dva</b> málʹčika</i> ― <span class="e-translation">two boys</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">two of a boy</span>”)</div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>две</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́ги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dve</b> knígi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">two books</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">two of a book</span>”)</div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пятьдесят.html>пятьдеся́т</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчика</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pjatʹdesját <b>dva</b> málʹčika</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fifty-two boys</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">fifty-two of a boy</span>”)</div></li></ul></dd></dl>
<ul><li><i>In the nominative case, all nouns become genitive singular. In the accusative case, animate nouns become genitive plural and inanimate nouns remain in genitive singular.</i></li></ul>
<dl><dd><ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>Две</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ки</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кот.html>кота́</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>две</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́ги</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:журнал.html>журна́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свалиться.html>свали́лись</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>стола́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Dve</b> sobáki, <b>dva</b> kotá, <b>dve</b> knígi i <b>dva</b> žurnála svalílisʹ so stolá.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Two dogs, two cats, two books and two journals fell from the table.</span></dd></dl></div> (<i>"<a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a>" transforms all nouns from nominative to genitive singular.</i>)</li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:видеть.html>ви́жу</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>двух</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́к</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>двух</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кот.html>кото́в</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>две</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́ги</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:журнал.html>журна́ла</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja vížu <b>dvux</b> sobák, <b>dvux</b> kotóv, <b>dve</b> knígi i <b>dva</b> žurnála.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I see two dogs, two cats, two books and two journals.</span></dd></dl></div> (<i>The verb "<a href = vnd.unilang:видеть.html>ви́жу</a>" governs accusative case, and "<a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a>" transforms dogs and cats from accusative to genitive plural.</i>)</li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:скачать.html>скача́л</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:редактор.html>редактора</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пригласить.html>пригласи́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обед.html>обе́д</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>двух</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:редактор.html>редакторов</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja skačál <b>dva</b> redaktora i priglasíl na obéd <b>dvux</b> redaktorov.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I downloaded two editors and invited two editors for lunch.</span></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">Заземлив <b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:проводник.html>проводника́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:электрик.html>эле́ктрик</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спасти.html>спас</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>двух</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:проводник.html>проводнико́в</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Zazemliv <b>dva</b> provodniká, eléktrik spas <b>dvux</b> provodnikóv.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Grounding the two (electrical) conductors, the electrician saved the two (train) conductors.</span></dd></dl></div></li></ul></dd></dl>
<ul><li><i>The reason behind the <b>genitive singular</b> here is that, in Old Russian, </i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a></b><i> governed the dual number, and the old <b>nominative dual</b> form was the same as the masculine <b>genitive singular</b>. When the dual number was lost in Russian, the form came to be considered the genitive singular that it resembled. This was extended to include the numbers </i><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tri</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span><i> and </i><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:четыре.html>четы́ре</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">četýre</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span><i>, and eventually it was applied by analogy to feminine nouns as well.</i></li>
<li><i>While the noun in a nominative construction is in the <b>genitive singular</b> following <b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a></b> or <b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>две</a></b>, an intervening adjective or adjectival participle will be in the <b>genitive plural</b> or <b>nominative plural</b> </i>
<ul><li><i>If <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a> is in nominative case, the adjective will be nominative plural when the noun is feminine</i></li></ul></li></ul>
<dl><dd><ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тут.html>Тут</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>две</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ки</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>больших</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кот.html>кота́</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>две</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́ги</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>больших</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>стола́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Tut <b>dve</b> bolʹšije sobáki, <b>dva</b> bolʹšix kotá, <b>dve</b> bolʹšije knígi i <b>dva</b> bolʹšix stolá.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Here are two big dogs, two big cats, two big books and two big tables.</span></dd></dl></div></li></ul></dd></dl>
<ul><li><ul><li><i>If <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a> is in accusative case, the adjective will be the same as the nominative plural only if the noun is feminine inanimate</i></li></ul></li></ul>
<dl><dd><ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:видеть.html>ви́жу</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>двух</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>больших</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́к</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>двух</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>больших</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кот.html>кото́в</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>две</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́ги</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>больших</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>стола́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja vížu <b>dvux</b> bolʹšix sobák, <b>dvux</b> bolʹšix kotóv, <b>dve</b> bolʹšije knígi i <b>dva</b> bolʹšix stolá.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I see two big dogs, two big cats, two big books and two big tables.</span></dd></dl></div></li></ul></dd></dl>
<ul><li><ul><li>Another way of seeing this is:</li></ul></li></ul>
<dl><dd><ul><li>Nominative feminine is <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>две</a> + nominative plural adjective + genitive singular noun</li>
<li>Nominative masculine is <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a> + genitive plural adjective + genitive singular noun.</li>
<li>Cases other than nominative and accusative (genitive, dative, instrumental, and prepositional) use plural forms, and agree in number and case with the noun.</li>
<li>Accusative animate is the same as the genitive, and accusative inanimate is the same as the nominative.</li></ul></dd></dl>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>Три</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">Tri</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:четыре.html>четы́ре</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">četýre</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> obey the same rules.</li></ul>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b> </b>
</p><p>Числительное, <a href = vnd.unilang:количественный.html>коли́чественное</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:порядковый.html>поря́дковое</a> числительное — <a href = vnd.unilang:второй.html>второ́й</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:собирательный.html>собира́тельные</a> числительные — <a href = vnd.unilang:двое.html>дво́е</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:оба.html>о́ба</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-дв-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двадцатилетний.html>двадцатиле́тний</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dvadcatilétnij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> twenty-year
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:двадцатилетний.html>двадцатиле́тнее</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:царствование.html>ца́рствование</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dvadcatilétneje</b> cárstvovanije</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>twenty-year</b> reign</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>twenty-year-old
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:двадцатилетний.html>двадцатиле́тняя</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:женщина.html>же́нщина</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dvadcatilétnjaja</b> žénščina</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a woman <b>of twenty</b>; a <b>twenty-year-old</b> woman</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***двадцать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:двадцать.html>два́дцать</a> (407)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-дцать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-dcatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or "twice ten". This was an <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small> dual form.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двадцать.html>два́дцать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dvádcatʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>twenty (20)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:двадцать.html>два́дцать</a></strong></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dvadcatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in the nominative case and accusative case governs the genitive plural of the noun. In other cases, it governs the corresponding plural case of the noun.
</p>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:двадцать.html>два́дцать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dvádcatʹ</b> málʹčikov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">twenty boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:двадцать.html>двадцатью́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиками</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>dvadcatʹjú</b> málʹčikami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">with twenty boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:двадцать.html>два́дцать</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">málʹčikov <b>dvádcatʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">approximately twenty boys</span></div></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>дцать</b>
</p><p>Числительное, <a href = vnd.unilang:количественный.html>коли́чественное</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:порядковый.html>поря́дковое</a> числительное — <a href = vnd.unilang:двадцатый.html>двадца́тый</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-дв-</b>; интерфикс: <b>-а-</b>; суффикс: <b>-дцать</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дважды.html>два́жды</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dváždy</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>twice, on two occasions
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дважды.html>два́жды</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жи́зни</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dváždy</b> v žízni</i> ― <span class="e-translation">twice in someone's life</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>2x, twice as much
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дважды.html>два́жды</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:десять.html>де́сять</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dváždy</b> pjatʹ — désjatʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>two times</b> five is ten</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***двенадцать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:двенадцать.html>двена́дцать</a> (1854)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compounded from <b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>две</a></b> + <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> + <b>дцать</b>, or <i>two on ten</i>. The feminine <b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>две</a></b> is used here because the final syllable <b>дцать</b>, an old short form of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:десять.html>де́сять</a></b>, is a feminine substantive.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двенадцать.html>двена́дцать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dvenádcatʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>twelve (12)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:двенадцать.html>двена́дцать</a></strong></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dvenadcatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in the nominative case and accusative case governs the genitive plural of the noun. In other cases, it governs the corresponding plural case of the noun.
</p>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:двенадцать.html>двена́дцать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dvenádcatʹ</b> málʹčikov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">twelve boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:двенадцать.html>двена́дцатью</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиками</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>dvenádcatʹju</b> málʹčikami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">with twelve boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:двенадцать.html>двена́дцать</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">málʹčikov <b>dvenádcatʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">approximately twelve boys</span></div></li></ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дверь.html>дверь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dverʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

***дверь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дверь.html>дверь</a> (141)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dvьrь</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰwer-</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">door</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дверь.html>дверь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dverʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дверь.html>две́ри</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дверь.html>две́ри</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дверь.html>двере́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>door
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дверь.html>дверя́х</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>dverjáx</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">in the doorway</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:политика.html>поли́тика</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:открытый.html>откры́тых</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дверь.html>двере́й</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">polítika otkrýtyx <b>dveréj</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">open-door policy</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:закрытый.html>закры́тых</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дверь.html>дверя́х</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pri zakrýtyx <b>dverjáx</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">behind closed doors<i>; </i>in private</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дверь.html>дверь</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 3-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 8e^  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***двести.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:двести.html>две́сти</a> (1997)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>An Old East Slavic dual form from the Old Church Slavic dual <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">двѣстѣ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dvěstě</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двести.html>две́сти</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dvésti</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>two hundred (200)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><b><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двести.html>две́сти</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dvésti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></b> in the nominative case governs the genitive plural of the noun.
</p>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:двести.html>две́сти</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dvésti</b> málʹčikov</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>two hundred</b> boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:двести.html>две́сти</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">málʹčikov <b>dvésti</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">approximately <b>two hundred</b> boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:двести.html>две́сти</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́г</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dvésti</b> knig</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>two hundred</b> books</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>они́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́х</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:двести.html>двухста́х</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:солдат.html>солда́тах</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oní govoríli o svoíx <b>dvuxstáx</b> soldátax.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">They were talking about their <b>two hundred</b> soldiers.</span></div></li></ul>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

</p>
